## Brand Guidelines

### 2014

**Logo Information:**

- Red Bull Branding Logo: Used in upper left-hand corner, serves as website favicon (16px x 16px). Dimensions: 50px x 76px. Padding left: 0. Location: 'Main Bar'.
- Red Bull TV Logo: Website Dimensions 50px x 76px, Original logo size at location 'Module 3-Up'.
- RedBull.COM Logo: Dimensions and Top Margin: 159px. Location: 'Footer Main Navigation'. Website icon link redirects to homepage.

**Color Information:**

- Red Bull Red: CMYK: 14, 100, 66, 2; RGB: 204, 31, 75; HEX: CC1E4A. Used for headlines.
- Outrageous Orange: CMYK: 0, 60, 100, 0; RGB: 245, 129, 32; HEX: F4801F. Used in the logo.
- Sunbelt Yellow: CMYK: 0, 20, 100, 0; RGB: 255, 202, 6; HEX: FFC906. Used in the logo.

**Typography Information:**

- Kremlin: Title for 'Follow Red Bull' Social Media Icons. Color: #FFFFFF. Sizes: 20px. Line height: 41px.
- Red Bull Siri Bold: For headers and hyperlinks. Colors: #CC14A; #FFFFFF. Sizes: 30px, 20px, 25px, 14px, 22px.
- Red Bull Core-Bold: For hyperlinks and small headers. Colors: #CC14A; #FFFFFF. Sizes: 30px, 20px, 25px, 14px, 22px.
- Red Bull Siri: Used for body copy. Color: #000000. Sizes: 15.5px, 12.2px.

**Imagery Photography:**
